 Lok sabha chunav Exit poll 2019 apane aakhri daur main pahunch chukaa he or 19 may ko antim charan kii voting ke baad agsit pole aane shuru ho jaaenge
 All the eyes on these polls, which predict the win-loss before the results, are fixed
 agsit pole, opinian pole kaa hi hissaa he
 But the method of extracting data from both is different
 aaie jaanate hai inamen kya fark hota he or kaise ye matadaataaon se unki raay lene main kaam karte hai?kya hota he opinian pole?opinian pole sidhe voter se judaa hota he
 In this, data are collected in different ways to understand public opinion
 yani logon se baat karne, unki raay jaanane ke tareeke alag-alag apanaae jate hai
 Pre poll, exit poll and post poll are 3 branches of Opinion poll
 par zyaadaatar log agsit pole (exit Poll) or post pole (post poll) ko ek hi samaj lete hai, lekin aisa nahin he
 These two are completely different from each other
 pre pole kya hota he?kisi bhi chunaav kii ghoshnaa or voting se pehle jo survey aap tivi main dekhte hai yaa akhabaaron main padhate hai ki agar aaj chunaav hue to kis party kii sarkaar banegi, yah pre pole hota he
 For example, suppose Lok Sabha elections 2019 will be held in seven phases from 11 April to 19 May
 chunaav kii ghoshnaa 11 march ko hui thi
 After which TV channels or newspapers told that if elections are held today, which party will get how many seats
 yah pre pole se hi tay hota he
 Lok Sabha Elections 2019: know what are exit polls, how are the figures called exit polls? Exit Poll is always on voting day
 agsit pole main matdaan dene ke turant baad jab voter poling booth se baahar nikalataa he to usase kuch sawaal karke uskaa man tatola jaataa he
 It is then analyzed
 ise agsit pole kehete hai
 Its data is submitted on the day of voting, then the exit poll is shown on the evening of the last voting day
 post pole main kya tay hota he?post pole ke parinaam zyada sateek hote hai
 In the exit poll, soon after the polling, the survey agency gets a rough account of the opinion of the voter
 jabaki post pole hameshaa matdaan ke agle din yaa phir ek-do din baad hote hai
 For example, suppose the sixth phase of voting took place on 12 May
 to survey karne vaali agency matadaataaon se 13, 14, yaa 15 may tak unki raay jaan lee hogi, ise post pole kaha jaataa he
 Who should trust? The simple answer is post poll
 agar aap aankadon par jaaen to sampling sabase zyada myne rakhti he
 On this basis, it can be said that Exit Poll is more likely to be wrong than Pre Poll or Post Poll because in the process of Exit Poll, the scientific methods which are adopted in Post Poll or Pre Poll are not used
 
 lok sabha chunaav 2019: kaise hote hai agsit pole or post pole survey, kya he sample lene kii prakriyaakyon he zyada sateek, aise samajhie?post pole ke jariye janata kii raay jaanane main sabase bada kaam field work kaa hota he
 For its sampling, employees of the poll survey agency meet the common people and know their opinion
 is prakriya main jin logon ko shaamil kiya jaataa he unhen ek form bharne ko diya jaataa he
 So that the identity of the voters remains secret and they feel free to give their opinion
 is form ko ek silband dibbe main rakh jaataa he
 Sampling is most important in post poll
 post pole voting ke ek-do din baad hote hai
 Whereas in exit polls, voters are consulted on the day of voting
 is vidha main poling booth par voters se raay jaani jaati he, jabaki opinian pole ke liye agency ke log gaanvon, kasbe, jile str par logon se raay lene jate hai
 In such a situation, the voters do not panic
 wo jise vot de chukaa he uske naam kaa parchaa dibbe main daal detaa he

 Security researchers have started to point out Android's security flaws
 iske tahat yah paaya gaya ki ataikars mobile or wifai ke bich ke trephic ko pard sakate hai or agar chahen to isamen badlaav karke website main mailaware inject kar sakate hai
 Now tell it to you in easy words
 darasal wifai router se mobile tak data packets ke rup main travel karte hai
 Usually these data are encrypted so that even if a hacker intercepts them, it cannot know what is in this packet
 lekin agar wifai router se mobile main internet conect he or ataikar wifai se aapke divaais ke bich hi trephic ko pard le or use ye pataa chale kii aap internet par kya kar rahe hai to ye vaaki kai lihaaj se khatarnaak he
 Mathie vanhoff of the Belgian KU Leuven University says, 'this attack can be done on all modern protected wifi networks, the weakness is in the wifi standard and not in any particular product'
 is tarah ke atake ko kii ri instolation atake yani KRACK kaha jaataa he or iske tahat havers ancrypted wifai network kii bhi jaankariyaan pard lete hai or samvedansheel jaankariyaan chura sakate hai
 According to the researchers, such flaws are highest in Android and Linux based devices
 daawa kiya gaya he ki aise atex nae wifai par bhi kiye ja sakate hai jinamein WPA yaa WPA 2 kii ancripshan hoti he
 This weakness is only in the wifi standard which can affect the entire Windows, Mac OS, ios, Linux OS including Android
 abhi tak ye mana jaataa he ki wifai ke jariye joinformation transfar hote hai wo sicyor or ancryptexote hai
 But by intercepting traffic, attackers or hackers can get information about what is in it
 iske liye ek divaais kii jarurat hoti he jise havers istemaal karte hai or isse credit card number, password, chat massej, photose, email or duusare tarah ke online communication chori kiye ja sakate hai
 Sirchers have claimed that 41 percent of Android devices have found this flaw, causing a wifi attack on them
 jaisaa aapako pehle bataaya wifai atake ke gambhir nuksaan ho sakate hai
 Since hackers can intercept wifi traffic only, they also have the option to inject many other dangerous malware
 udhaaharan ke taur par wo intercept kiye gaye wifai trephic main badlaav karke aapke smartphone ko hack kar sakate hai, rancemaware inject kar sakate hai yaa website main mailaware daal sakate hai jisase aap gambhir pareshaani main aa sakate hai
 Android is Google's operating system, so the question is from Google
 apok bataa den ki google kaa kahana he ki company is khami ke bare main jaanati he or agle hafte main aise divaais main ptch apadet degi jisamen yah khami he
 Researchers believe that you cannot avoid such an attack even by changing the password of wifi
 lekin companiyon ne ise fiks karnaa shuru kiya he isliye yugers ko apane router kaa formaware apedat karan lenaa chahie
